status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"

status: publish

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>

categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>

categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">

<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>

<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"

status: publish

<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck

<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>

categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">

<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>

categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>

<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"

status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>

<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>

<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"

status: publish

<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila

date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"

status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>

categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-

title: Talk to the rubber duck


<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>
<p>But, sometimes I prefer <a title="Thinking Out Loud" href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?ThinkingOutLoud" target="_blank">thinking out loud</a>. It  works too and I recomend.</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde

<p><em>"Place a rubber duck on your monitor and describe your problems to it.  There's something magical about stating your problems aloud that makes  the solution more clear." - </em><a href="http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking" target="_blank">http://www.c2.com/cgi/wiki?RubberDucking</a></p>
<p>Nokia gave us rubber ducks at last <a title="Akademy 2010" href="http://akademy.kde.org" target="_blank">Akademy</a>. I loved it.</p>
<p>Now I have two <a title="Rubber ducking" href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck" target="_blank">ducks</a> to talk while programming:</p>
<p style="text-align:center;">
<p>[caption id="attachment_136" align="aligncenter" width="300" caption="Rubber ducking"]<a href="http://developer.qt.nokia.com/duck"><img class="size-medium wp-image-136 " title="Rubber ducking" src="/assets/images/14072010093.jpg?w=300" alt="Rubber ducking" width="300" height="224" /></a>[/caption]</p>,-
author: Camila
categories: Archives, Nerdices, Nonsense, Personal/Pessoal, poo, Programming
date: "2010-07-14T10:50:47Z"
 
published: true
status: publish
tags: akademy, ducks, kde
